# Roadmap

Version-by-version history of `adam`, grouped into two architectural eras. The final entry (v1.0.0) is the MVP cut.

## Lifecycle view

```
  v0.1.0 ────────────────── v0.4.0           v0.4.5 ──────────────── v1.0.0
  ├─ transformer era ───────────┤            ├─ FST + dialog era ────────┤
  │                              │            │                            │
  corpus curation                │            deterministic FST morphology │
  BPE tokenizer                  │            14 k-entry pure Kazakh Lexicon
  24.2 M transformer             │            25-intent dialog pipeline    │
  (archived as reference)        │            trilingual input, KZ output  │
                                 v            FST-guaranteed morphology    v
                              pivot                                       MVP
```

The transformer era (v0.1–v0.4) established the corpus, tokenizer, and training infrastructure. The FST + dialog era (v0.4.5+) replaced the stochastic model with a deterministic pipeline that holds predictability as a hard constraint. The v0.4.0 checkpoint is preserved in `data/training/` as a regression reference but is not on the v1.0.0 codepath.

## Phase 10 — FST + dialog layer (v0.4.5 → v1.0.0)

The MVP path. Each release is strictly additive — no rollbacks, no feature gating.

| Release | Scope | Result |
|---|---|---|
| v0.4.5 | `adam-kernel-fst` crate — phonology + morphotactics + parser + lexicon + CLI | 55 unit tests, 100% roundtrip on 36,238 full-lexicon cycles |
| v0.5.0 | Participles, converbs, vowel-final-stem aorist coalescence | 68 unit tests; most non-finite Kazakh verb forms covered |
| v0.5.5 | Pure Kazakh lexicon — drop 1,500 loanwords, add 500 Abai-attested classical roots | 14,106 entries, Abai coverage 88.8% → 97.8% |
| v0.6.0 | Derivational morphology — 11 word-formation suffixes | 78 unit tests; root→derived→inflected chains work end-to-end |
| v0.7.0 | First dialog layer — `adam-dialog` crate, 5-intent MVP, `adam_chat` CLI | 175 workspace tests; 5-layer predictable pipeline |
| v0.7.5 | Dialog widening to 10 intents; templates moved to `data/dialog/templates/v1.toml` | 183 workspace tests; data-driven template repo |
| v0.8.0 | 25 intents (+15: age, location, occupation, family, weather, time, compliment, request, well-wishes, statement-of-name); PersonName extraction | 201 workspace tests; first entity extraction lands |
| v0.8.5 | Multi-turn session state via `Conversation`; greeting `{name}` variants | 204 workspace tests; "Say your name once, get greeted forever" |
| v0.9.0 | Full entity absorption — Kazakh numeral parser (1–99), ablative/locative city, 1sg-copula occupation; `{age}/{city}/{occupation}` slots | 215 workspace tests; every statement contributes a remembered entity |
| v0.9.5 | FST-backed slot expansion — `{slot\|features}` parsed and rendered via `synthesise_noun`; cross-slot templates | 229 workspace tests; agreement becomes FST-guaranteed |
| v0.9.6 | Multilingual recogniser — Kazakh / Russian / English triggers for all 25 intents; Latin-root safety guard | 245 workspace tests |
| v0.9.7 | Lexicon-backed occupation recognition via generic 1sg-copula stripping + POS lookup | 251 workspace tests |
| v0.9.8 | Full slot syntax (Derivation + Possessive) + Latin→Cyrillic transliteration + triple-slot templates | 265 workspace tests; demo-ready UX |
| v0.9.9 | FST Instrumental harmony fix (`Алматыман → Алматымен`, `мұғалімбен → мұғаліммен`); 6 regression tests; template polish | 271 workspace tests; last stretch before MVP |
| v1.0.0 | **MVP cut** — no new features; full documentation refresh; transformer-era narrative compressed into history section | 271 workspace tests; investor-demoable |
| v1.1.0 | **Kazakh-only revert + modern Lexicon + smart Unknown** — reverted v0.9.6 multilingual triggers, removed transliteration module; added Insult intent; Unknown handler extracts noun hint via FST; +12 modern Kazakh Lexicon roots | 253 workspace tests; course-correction toward thinking Kazakh model |
| v1.1.5 | **Corpus audit baseline** — new `corpus_audit` binary measures the v1.x starting position per-source: word counts, vocab, Kazakh purity, dedup. Reports **2.24 M words baseline** (45× expansion needed to reach the 100 M target). Adds expansion plan through v1.5.0 | 256 workspace tests; measurable progress toward thinking model |
| v1.2.0 | **Classical literature expansion** — new `kazakh_classics_pack.json` (111 samples, 926 words, **100.00 % Kazakh purity**) from Ыбырай Алтынсарин + Мағжан Жұмабаев (kk.wikisource, public domain). OCR deferred | 256 workspace tests; literary core added |
| v1.3.0 | **Wikipedia re-extract** — rewrote `process_wikipedia_kz` (byte-by-byte → 64 KB chunked streaming, 100× faster; added 10 % loanword-density filter). Committed pack: 150 k samples / 1.61 M words / 99.99 % purity. Local uncapped: 1.4 M samples / 15 M words. Corpus total 2.85 M words, expansion gap 45× → 35× | 256 workspace tests; +27 % corpus |
| v1.3.5 | **Sharding + docs drift + v2.0 direction committed** — `--full` mode writes 10 shards (≤50 MB each) to gitignored `data/curated/shards/` for local retrieval-engine fuel; `corpus_audit --local` scans them. Docs fixed: badge 253→256, `foundation_scope` no longer claims trilingual/transliteration, "FST-guaranteed" wording tightened. **v2.0 committed as retrieval-over-corpus, not a trained LM** | 256 workspace tests; local corpus 16 M words, gap to 100 M = 6.2× |
| v1.4.0 | **FST-NER + DST + predicate-copula FST** — added `Predicate` feature to `NounFeatures` (7 person variants + 6 suffix templates); +30 Kazakh place-name entries in Lexicon; `detect_statement_of_location` / `detect_statement_of_occupation` refactored to use `Analysis` as primary path; `Conversation` gained `active_intent` + `intent_history` + `resolve_follow_up` | 262 workspace tests; closes Codex/Antigravity critiques |
| v1.4.5 | **Lexicon polish +20 nouns** — modern Kazakh professions (нұсқаушы, кеңесші, жетекші, жүргізуші, саудагер, …) and common conversational vocabulary (әке, аға, апа, бүгін, ертең, кеше, мекеме, кеңсе, ұйым). All native Kazakh, no loanwords | 262 workspace tests; each new profession round-trips through FST-NER |
| v1.5.0 | **CC-100 re-extract** — rewrote `process_cc100_kk` (stdin streaming, old 50 k cap removed, 10 % loanword-density filter, sharding at 140 k samples/shard). Committed pack: 140 k samples / 4.01 M words committed. 33 local shards (02–34) add 4.6 M samples / 74 M more local words. **Corpus: 4.01 M committed / 77.9 M local; gap to 100 M = 1.3×**. Purity −1.6 pp (web-crawl tax, accepted per corpus-purity directive) | 262 workspace tests; +27× local corpus |
| v1.5.5 | **Morpheme-coverage audit** — new `morpheme_coverage` binary. Prefix-matches every committed word against the 14,247-root Lexicon, reports per-pack coverage + top 20 uncovered words by frequency. Baseline: **79.48 % across 3.84 M committed words** (synthetic 99.82 %, real-corpus packs 76–81 %). Concrete Lexicon gaps identified: `деп`, `осы`, `оның`, `деген`, `пен`, `орта`. v1.5.5 was originally planned as "government sources"; that directive moves to v1.6.x since the sources need dedicated scraping infrastructure | 267 workspace tests; coverage delta now a measurable PR metric |
| v1.6.0 | **Retrieval engine bootstrap** — new `adam-retrieval` crate with `MorphemeIndex` (BTreeMap for deterministic JSON) + `SampleRef` + `search` + `search_conjunction`. New `build_morpheme_index` binary parses committed packs through the FST (unique-word cache → ~10 min full-corpus build). Two modes: default `--limit 500/pack` writes the committed 1.6 MB snapshot; `--full` writes the gitignored 700 MB full index. FST throughput measured at 1.155 ms/word. No `Intent::Unknown` integration yet (v1.6.5+) | 274 workspace tests; retrieval crate shipped |
| v1.6.5 | **Retrieval wired into Intent::Unknown** — `MorphemeIndex` gains `sample_texts` so dialog can cite the actual sentence, not just the sample id. `Conversation::with_morpheme_index` attaches the index; when Unknown fires with a recognised noun, the response quotes a verbatim corpus example. New `unknown.with_evidence` template family wraps quotes in «…». Deterministic: picks the first (sorted) posting — reproducible across runs. No regression: without an index, v1.1.0 noun-echo behaviour is preserved | 279 workspace tests; dialog now cites Abai, Wikipedia, CC-100 for its fallback turns |
| v1.7.0 | **Deterministic retrieval ranking** — `MorphemeIndex::rank` replaces "first posting" with a composite score: **0.40·overlap + 0.30·pack_purity + 0.15·length_goodness − 0.15·loanword_density**. Dialog ranks over every content root (`content_roots`), not just the first. Editorial pack priors hardcode classical > curated > Wikipedia > web. Visible effect: «мектеп керек пе» now cites an 8-word sentence instead of a 36-word bureaucratic paragraph. Zero randomness, zero training; ties break by `(pack, sample_id)` | 286 workspace tests; retrieval engine starts behaving like a search engine |
| v1.8.0 | **Session-aware compositional synthesis (option A: frame-only)** — retrieved quote stays verbatim (zero fabrication risk); frame around it becomes session-aware. When user has `name`/`city`/`age`/`occupation` remembered, planner prefers a template that personalises the citation («Сіз, Дәулет, бала туралы сұрап тұрсыз ба…» instead of just «бала туралы…»). Implemented as pure templates — no planner logic change, no new crate. `template_is_fillable` auto-activates session-aware variants when slots exist. Known bug: `-мын` greedy-strip in occupation recogniser (v1.8.5 fix) | 288 workspace tests; composition implemented as pure data |
| v1.8.5 | **Locative+P1Sg bug fix + FST-aware city slots + README refresh** — fixed `detect_statement_of_occupation` to reject Locative/Ablative cases (so «мен Алматыдамын» → `city: Алматы`, not `occupation: алматы`); `detect_statement_of_location` now accepts bare Locative+P1Sg without requiring a separate verb. Wired `{city|locative}` into 2 retrieval templates so «Алматыда тұратын сізге…» renders with harmony-correct locative suffix (no more dangling `Алматы-да`). Comprehensive README refresh bringing all version refs, badges, capabilities, specs, history and out-of-scope lists in sync with the v1.5.0–v1.8.0 retrieval-era arc | 290 workspace tests; +2 regression tests |
| v1.9.0 | **In-sample city swap (option B, opt-in, year-guarded)** — new `adam-retrieval::compose` module with `compose_with_city(sample, user_city, lexicon)` → `Composition` carrying provenance per `Swap`. Closed editorial list `PLACE_NAMES` (20 Kazakh cities); user's city must also be in the list. Biographical-year guard refuses the whole swap on any 4-digit year in [1500, 2100] to keep biographies untouched. New `ComposeMode { Verbatim, InSampleCitySwap }` on `Conversation` with `with_compose_mode(...)` — default stays `Verbatim` (v1.8.5 behaviour, byte-identical corpus quote). `InSampleCitySwap` rewrites city mentions inside the cited quote to the user's city via FST feature-preserving synthesis. Grammaticality FST-guaranteed, semantic truthfulness no longer guaranteed — option B trade-off is explicit and auditable | 301 workspace tests; +8 compose unit + +3 dialog e2e |
| v1.9.5 | **Composition-marker framing (adapted-evidence family)** — restores the traceability contract broken in v1.9.0. `Intent::Unknown` gains `example_adapted: bool`; when `true` the planner routes to the new `unknown.with_adapted_evidence` family whose every template contains the «бейімд-» stem («бейімделген нұсқа», «қалаңызға бейімдеп көрдім»). `maybe_compose` now returns `(String, bool)` so the swap flag propagates cleanly. Two trust-critical tests enforce: (a) swap → marker fires, (b) no swap → marker NEVER fires — no false claims of adaptation. The user can always distinguish a verbatim corpus quote from an adapted one by grepping for «бейімд-» | 303 workspace tests; +2 e2e guarantees |
| v2.0.0 | **v2.0 commitment release — investor-demoable** — not a feature drop, an architectural commitment: `project_retrieval_not_neural_v2` is now frozen. New `adam_demo` scripted 15-turn walkthrough (3 parts — verbatim, opt-in swap with guards, synthetic swap showing the marker). `adam_chat` now auto-loads the morpheme index and exposes `--compose` / `--no-retrieval` flags. New `docs/architecture_v2.md` as single canonical reference. README gains a "Why adam" comparison table vs mainstream LLMs. Explicit commitments declared: not a trained model, not multilingual, not generative, not a generalist, not self-modifying | 303 tests pass (unchanged); 0 new tests — v2.0 adds binaries + docs on top of the v1.9.5 library surface |
| v2.1.0 | **ILMRR bootstrap — fact extraction** — first step toward reasoning. New `adam-reasoning` crate with typed `Fact { subject, predicate, object, pattern, source, confidence, raw_text }`. `Predicate` enum starts with `IsA` + `LivesIn`. `ConfidenceKind` is categorical evidence (Grammar, CuratedQuote, RepeatedPattern, HumanApproved, RuleInferred) — **not an LLM probability**. Two pattern matchers: copula `X — Y` with strict single-token LHS + head-extracted RHS (right-to-left FST scan resolves "Y-сі" → root Y); locative-existential `X Y-да тұрады` with `Case::Locative` + `тұру`-verb + bare-nominative subject. New `extract_facts` binary (default / `--full` / `--limit N` modes, streamed progress). Baseline on committed corpus: **11 facts from 3,191 samples, 7 precise + 4 Lexicon-gap signals** (байлық, жанашы, бастау, болашақ) → concrete v2.2 agenda. All facts provenance-carrying back to `(pack, sample_id)`. Zero regressions elsewhere | 325 workspace tests (+22 reasoning); first structured knowledge artifact `data/retrieval/facts.json` |
| v2.2.0 | **Lexicon pollution purge + `Has` predicate** — the v2.1 feedback loop paid off. Scan found **87 intervocalic-voicing-duplicate root pairs** in segmentation_roots.json (кітап↔кітаб, сабақ↔сабағ, болашақ↔болашағ …), all Apertium-import artefacts. Purged 87 + added 3 missing roots (байлық, бастау, жанашыр). Zero code references to any of the 87 IDs → no regressions. New third pattern matcher `possessive_has`: `X-тың Y-сы бар` → `Has` via `Case::Genitive` + `Possessive::P3` + existential `бар` + adjacency guard. New `Predicate::Has` variant. Extraction: 11→13 facts, 1→2 distinct predicates; 3 of 4 v2.1 imprecisions corrected (ынтымақ→байлық, бала→болашақ, ана→жанашыр); 1 remains (жер→бастау blocked by vowel-final+P3 FST bug, filed for v2.3). Lexicon delta: 4516→4432 roots (−84, cleaner) | 328 workspace tests (+3 possessive); 13 facts, 2 predicates |
| v2.3.0 | **FST glide-vowel fix + Lexical Graph v0** — Kazakh `у`, `и`, `ю` moved from `ConsonantClass::VowelPreceding` to `HighSonorant` (aligning code with enum docstring). Fixes vowel-final + P3 mis-synthesis: `оқу+P3` = оқуы (not оқусы), `бастау+P3` = бастауы. v2.2's last imprecision (жер → бастау) now resolves correctly. New `adam_reasoning::graph::LexicalGraph` — pure projection of `facts.json` into `(nodes, edges)` with provenance on every edge. `build_lexical_graph` binary emits `data/retrieval/lexical_graph.json`. Extraction delta: 13→**15 facts, 0 imprecisions**. Graph state: 29 nodes, 15 edges, most-connected `бұлақ` (degree 2). Zero regressions; 335 tests (+7 graph) | 335 workspace tests; 15 facts with 0 imprecisions + first lexical graph artifact |
| v2.4.0 | **Rule reasoner v0 (forward-chaining) + docs-currency audit** — new `adam_reasoning::reasoner` + `run_reasoner` binary. 1 active rule (`R1_is_a_transitivity`: A IsA B ∧ B IsA C ⟹ A IsA C), 4 documented for v2.5+. Every derived fact carries `rule_id`, non-empty `source_chain`, and `ConfidenceKind::RuleInferred` (never `Grammar`). Test-enforced trust invariants: derived ⇒ rule-inferred confidence; fixpoint reached ⇒ idempotent; tautology (A IsA A) never emitted. Honest baseline: **0 derivations on current 15 facts** — reasoner correctly wired (unit tests verify 3-hop chains), data doesn't yet form chains; v2.5 patterns will populate middle nodes. Plus: comprehensive docs-currency audit (13 files refreshed — Cargo descriptions, crate lib.rs docstrings, foundation_scope, corpus_audit, repository_layout, eval_baseline, architecture_v2, dialog README, lexicon README, dialog architecture history), new `feedback_docs_currency` memory codifies the per-release checklist | 343 workspace tests (+8 reasoner); first rule-inference artifact `data/retrieval/derived_facts.json` |
| v2.5.0 | **`GoesTo` predicate + dative-motion pattern (v3.0 ladder step 1/6)** — first rung of the committed v2.5 → v3.0 ladder toward investor-demoable intelligent MVP. New `Predicate::GoesTo`, new `patterns::dative_goes_to` (X Y-ке барады → GoesTo; type-checked on `Case::Dative` + verb root `бару` + bare-nominative subject; closed-class and tautology guards). `LexicalGraph::from_facts` now handles `goes_to` string; `unreachable!` arm enforces compile-time branch-completeness for future predicate variants. 0 firings on the committed 3191 samples (proverbs + metaphors rarely use dative-motion), pattern verified by 4 unit tests. Zero regressions | 347 workspace tests (+4 dative tests); 15 facts unchanged; graph and derived artefacts regenerated |
| v2.6.0 | **`PartOf` + `RelatedTo` predicates + R5 rule active (v3.0 ladder step 2/6)** — the reasoner starts producing real derivations. Two new predicate variants. R5 rule (`A IsA X ∧ B IsA X ⟹ RelatedTo(A, B)`, symmetric with canonical-pair dedup) activates. First real derivation on the v2.5 fact set: `кітап RelatedTo ілім` (both IsA бұлақ across two different proverbs → related). Graph projection handles both new predicate strings with the existing compile-time `unreachable!` safety arm. Zero regressions | 352 workspace tests (+5 R5 + predicate stability); derived_facts.json now contains 1 real inference |
| v2.7.0 | **Dialog integration: reasoning chains in `Intent::Unknown` (v3.0 ladder step 3/6)** — the reasoner's output becomes user-visible. `Conversation` gains `derived_facts` + `extracted_facts` fields + `with_reasoning_chains(...)` builder. `Intent::Unknown` gains `reasoning_chain: Option<String>`. Pure renderer `render_derivation_as_kazakh` produces Kazakh prose with the mandatory «байланыс-» trust marker. Planner routes to new `unknown.with_derived_chain` family (4 templates, all with «байланыс-») when a chain fires. `adam_chat` autoloads `facts.json` + `derived_facts.json` at startup. End-to-end demo: `adam_chat --once "кітап туралы бірдеңе айт"` → «кітап пен ілім бір-біріне байланысты екен». Test-enforced trust invariants: chain match ⇒ marker fires; no derived_facts ⇒ marker NEVER fires across 32 seeds (mirrors v1.9.5's verbatim-never-claims-adapted). Zero regressions | 354 workspace tests (+2 e2e); first user-visible inference in adam's history |
| v2.8.0 | **R2 Has-inheritance + complete predicate renderers (v3.0 ladder step 4/6)** — activates `R2_has_inheritance` (A IsA B ∧ B Has X ⟹ A Has X, tautology-guarded, `ConfidenceKind::RuleInferred` labelled for consumer-side monotonic-inheritance scepticism). Fills out `render_derivation_as_kazakh` — every `Predicate` variant (IsA, LivesIn, Has, GoesTo, PartOf, RelatedTo) now produces a specific Kazakh phrasing with the mandatory «байланыс-» marker; exhaustive match, no generic fallback. On current 15-fact corpus: R2 fires 0 (no outgoing Has edges from IsA targets — awaits pattern density from future releases). Zero regressions | 357 workspace tests (+3 R2); reasoner now carries 3 active rules (R1/R2/R5) with full predicate coverage |
| v2.9.0 | **Investor-demo polish: `adam_demo` Part 4 (v3.0 ladder step 5/6)** — the scripted walkthrough gains a fourth part loading committed `facts.json` + `derived_facts.json`, surfacing the derivation `кітап RelatedTo ілім` with full `source_chain` provenance (`proverb_003`, `cv_kk_00047`), running the user probe «кітап туралы бірдеңе айт» across 4 deterministic seeds — every response carries the «байланыс-» trust marker, tagged `[chain]` in the demo output for at-a-glance scanning. Banner bumped to "v2.9 — 4-part scripted demo (intents + retrieval + composition + reasoning)". Graceful no-op with help message if artefacts are missing. No library changes, no new tests — pure demo-binary polish | 357 workspace tests (unchanged); investor-ready walkthrough covering the full v2.5 → v2.8 arc in one binary |
| v4.52.5 | **Engineering hygiene + doc currency + weekly plan** — driven by external code review (Codex, 2026-05-05). Fixes broken release gate + ~15 numeric/version drifts across docs. No new behaviour, no new tests, pure hygiene. **(1)** Bumps 7 stale data manifests v4.37.0 → v4.52.5 (data/eval/*.json, data/tokenizer/*.json, data/training/baseline_training_manifest.json). `verify_release_version.sh 4.52.5` now green (was failing since ~v4.37.5). **(2)** Re-stamps every numeric claim to ground truth across docs: 969 tests, 33 intents (was 31 in README badge; v4.51.0 added StatementOfActivity + AskActivity), foundation 2089/2349/46/27175, p50 1.07 ms. **(3)** Adds `description` field to 5 crate Cargo.toml files: adam-kernel (L0 foundation), adam-tokenizer (Kazakh-aware tokenizer + segmentation), adam-corpus (corpus pipeline + suffix priors + root affinity), adam-eval (eval + benchmark harness + stack contracts), adam-retrieval (morpheme-indexed retrieval engine). **(4)** `data/world_core/README.md` surfaces live totals at the top of «Current scale» section; v4.11.7 per-domain breakdown explicitly marked historical-snapshot for change-tracking. `data/README.md` updated: 874/995/30 → 2089/2349/46; 15521 facts / 21415 derivations → 2349/27175. **(5)** Updates `docs/foundation_scope.md` test count claim 822@v4.22.5 → 969@v4.52.5; `docs/performance.md` + `docs/corpus_audit.md` headers re-stamped; `docs/kazakh_grammar/07_dialog_architecture.md:133` intent-taxonomy heading clarifies «v1.1.0 shipped set — 26 intents; current count 33 at v4.52.5». **(6)** New `docs/weekly_plan_2026-W19.md` — concrete day-by-day deliverables for W19 (2026-05-05 → 2026-05-11): v4.53.0 math gerund-clause parser → v4.53.5 context-aware clarify → session 6 transcript → v4.54.0 Lexicon + bridge-fact expansion → v4.54.5 clippy hygiene + workspace.lints policy → v4.55.0 metrics-currency CI gate (`scripts/check_metrics_currency.sh`). Aligned with `project_v4_direction` (no investors), `feedback_real_human_testing_with_memory`, `project_bridge_fact_leverage`. **Verification:** Workspace 969 passing unchanged; `verify_release_version.sh 4.52.5` green; foundation unchanged; fmt + build clean. Cadence: `.5` patch — pure hygiene (no code-path changes; CI invariant restored; doc drift erased). Stripe (11) — generative AI via agglutinative composition. | 969 (unchanged) |
| v4.52.0 | **Transcript-driven session 5 fixes — continuous-form activity + compound occupation + demonstrative math anaphora** — driven by 2026-05-05 user dialog test session 5. Four concrete gaps closed plus measurable improvement to single-utterance multi-slot capture (v4.x context-aware-dialog directive). **(1)** Continuous-form activity detection — new `CONTINUOUS_CONVERBS` array (8 stems: әзірлеп / жасап / жазып / зерттеп / құрастырып / айналысып / дамытып / құрып). Bigram match: when a converb token is found AND the next token starts with «жатыр» (covers «жатырмын» 1sg / «жатырмыз» 1pl), treat the converb as the verb position; walk back to extract object. **(2)** Two new activity-verb roots — «дамыту» (develop) + «құру» (build/establish); 4 surface forms added to `ACTIVITY_VERBS`: дамытамын / құрамын (finite) + дамытатын / құратын (participle). **(3)** `detect_occupation_in_compound(input, lexicon)` — new pure function in `semantics.rs`. Mirrors `detect_activity_in_compound`. Tokenises lowered input; calls `strip_copula_and_lookup_noun` against the lexicon for the priority path; falls back to a 15-entry fixed-table lookup when no lexicon is provided. Returns `Some(Some(root))` when a noun + 1sg-copula form is identifiable. **(4)** `Conversation::turn` secondary occupation scan — runs after primary intent absorption + activity scan. When primary intent is NOT `StatementOfOccupation` AND the session doesn't already have an `occupation` slot, calls `detect_occupation_in_compound`. Captures occupation into session + belief graph. Lets a single utterance like «Менің атым X, мен Y-мын ...» populate `name` + `occupation` + `activity` slots in one turn. **(5)** AskActivity self-recall extended — `detect_ask_activity` treats any «менің» + activity-participle stem as 1sg self-recall. New stems: дамытатын / әзірлейтін / жасайтын / жазатын / зерттейтін / құрастыратын. Pre-v4.52.0 only «істейтін» was matched. **(6)** Demonstrative math anaphora «бұл нәтиже» — `Conversation::turn` math anaphora resolver gains a third anaphora family alongside «алдыңғы» / «соңғы»: «бұл (есептеу )?нәтиже» with full case-suffix preservation (Acc / Dat). **Live REPL replay:** «Менің атым Дәулет, мен бағдарламашымын және өзімнің жасанды интеллект моделімді жасап жатырмын» → all three slots captured (was name-only); «Менің нені дамытатыным есіңізде ме?» → "Жасанды интеллект модел — сіздің қазіргі ісіңіз деп жадыма түсірдім" (was clarify); «Менің мамандығым қандай?» → "Менің білуімше, мамандығыңыз бағдарламашы" (was no-slot fallback); «Енді бұл нәтижені 4-ке бөліңіз» → 6 (was math_refusal). **Verification:** Workspace 969 passing unchanged; adam-dialog lib 301; live REPL 4/4 session-5 scenarios verified; foundation unchanged 2089/2349/46/27175; fmt + build clean. | v4.46.0 | **Stage B bundle 3 — canonical gold pairs + audit substrate** — two architectural primitives connecting the v4.45.5 training algorithm to the future v4.46.5+ production wiring. **(1)** `canonical_training_pairs_v0() -> Vec<TrainingPair>` — 15 hand-curated gold pairs covering 5 feature dimensions + the disambiguation scenarios that the v4.38.0 SearchGraph ranker tiers handle today (confidence axis × 3, subject-overlap × 3, object-overlap × 1, recency × 2, richness × 1, multi-signal interactions × 5). Returns `{ heuristic_top_idx, selector_top_idx, disagreement, score_gap }`. Stable-tie-break matches `select_top` semantics (first index wins on ties). | v4.45.5 | **Stage B bundle 2 — pairwise margin-perceptron training pipeline** — Stage B continues. v4.45.0 shipped the foundation (`SelectionWeights` + `extract_features` + `score` + `select_top`). v4.45.5 ships the training algorithm: pairwise margin perceptron that takes a list of gold `(positive, negative)` candidate pairs and tunes a `SelectionWeights` table until every pair satisfies `score(positive) ≥ score(negative) + margin` (or `max_epochs` elapse). Pure function, deterministic per `(initial, pairs, config)`. **Architectural fit:** discrete (no gradient graph, no library deps), inspectable (still ~28 bytes after training), deterministic (no random sampling, no SGD batching variance). Satisfies the thesis constraint «weights/learning OK if discrete, inspectable, cheap; reject only LLM internals». **(1)** `TrainingPair` struct — labelled gold pair (positive vs negative candidate). **(2)** `TrainingConfig` — three hyperparameters (`learning_rate / margin / max_epochs`); `default_v0` hand-tuned for v0 feature scale. **(3)** `TrainingStats` — `epochs_run / final_violations / converged` reporting. **(4)** `train_perceptron(initial, pairs, config) -> (SelectionWeights, TrainingStats)` — pure loop; per-epoch iterates pairs; failing pairs trigger update by `lr × (pos_feature - neg_feature)` per weight component; early-exit on zero violations. **(5)** Re-exports in lib.rs. **(6)** 11 new unit tests verify convergence on linearly-separable data, determinism, no-op when pre-converged, max-epoch reporting, empty-pair handling, single-dimension signal pickup (recency / confidence), zero-lr no-progress, multi-signal convergence within budget, post-training rank correctness, epoch-count reporting, default-config stability. **(7)** NOT YET in v4.45.5 — real training data pipeline from canonical evals + REPL transcripts, audit-only wiring (compute selection scores at SearchGraph result point + log disagreement), production routing replacement of heuristic top-1 ranker. **Stage B status:** v4.45.0 — bundle 1 — foundation ✓; v4.45.5 — bundle 2 — training pipeline ✓; v4.46.0+ — bundle 3 — real training data + audit-only wiring; v4.50.0 (target) — bundle 4 — trained-weights replacement of heuristic ranker. **Verification:** Workspace **936 passing** (was 925; +11 training tests); adam-dialog lib **269 passing** (+11); selection module 24/24 (13 v4.45.0 + 11 v4.45.5); live REPL byte-identical to v4.45.0 (no production wiring yet); foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. | v4.43.9 | **`multiword_entity_hint` inflected-FIRST-word pass (architectural cleanup)** — closes the v4.43.8 architectural carry-forward. v4.43.8 fixed the «Қазіргі Қазақстан президенті» routing by registering both bare-form AND Gen-form variants of office phrases as multiwords — solved the symptom but registering parallel Gen-form variants is data-drift waiting to happen. v4.43.9 lifts the fix to the matcher itself. **(1)** Third pass in `multiword_entity_hint` — for 2-word entities `X Y`, accepts input `X{Gen} T` where T starts with Y's first 3 chars and X{Gen} is X + one of the six Kazakh genitive suffixes (-ның/-нің/-дың/-дің/-тың/-тің). | v4.22.0 | **Runtime integration of chain_tiebreak_root: priors+root infrastructure now reaches live dialog** — first minor in v4.22+ runtime-integration arc. v4.19.0→v4.21.5 built the eval framework + root priors + closed-class boost + FST paradigm matcher, closing eval at 100% across 23 cases. **But that 100% only applied inside the eval binary.** The actual dialog runtime was still using chain-only smoothed scoring without the root tiebreak. v4.22.0 closes the loop. **(1)** Runtime comparator in parse_input_inner extended — chain-prior re-rank gains a root-tiebreaker tier (chain_diff < EPSILON → score_root decides). | v4.15.0 | **First compositional ML layer: P(suffix_chain) priors + offline training pass** — first minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. The Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition (`root + suffix^n`). Pre-v4.15.0 the FST analyser had no distributional signal over which chains are actually common in Kazakh. v4.15.0 adds it as a frozen prior. **Infrastructure-only release**: the prior is loaded but not yet integrated into runtime decision-making — splitting the architectural addition from the behaviour change keeps both reversible. **Architectural addition:** new module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/suffix_priors.rs` (~280 lines + 8 tests). `struct SuffixPriors { version, trained_on_tokens, chain_log_prob }`. `from_counts` uses add-one Laplace smoothing; `score_noun`/`score_verb` are single hashmap probes. Unseen chains return `min_observed - ln(2)` so they rank strictly below the rarest observed chain. Schema-versioned (v1 at v4.15.0); loader rejects mismatched versions. **Training pass:** new binary `crates/adam-corpus/src/bin/train_suffix_priors.rs`. Walks `data/curated/*.json` packs, FST-analyses each token, attributes uniform `1/N` weight to each candidate (unbiased given no labels), writes `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` deterministically (sorted keys, byte-stable across runs). Why uniform attribution: first-parse weighting would make the prior a circular reflection of existing tie-breaking; uniform attribution captures which chains *appear at all* in real Kazakh text. Per user's directive (`project_v4_direction`): Predictable (no embeddings/SGD), Cheap (~5min training, hashmap probe at runtime), Safe (only ranks existing parses, never invents), Foundation (preserves `корень + функция^n`, version-bump path built in). Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 frozen artifact + new dep edge `adam-corpus → adam-kernel-fst`. **Cadence: minor.** Stripe (4) — compositional ML — opens. Next: v4.15.5 (runtime integration as tiebreaker), v4.16.0 (context-aware priors `P(chain | preceding_chain)`). | 793 (+8 suffix_priors unit tests) |

| v4.13.5 | **Capability honest fallbacks: generic verb-capability + multi-topic capability detection** — patch in the v4.12+ humanness arc closing the two known gaps explicitly listed in the v4.13.0 release notes. **(1)** New `SystemAspect::GenericCapability` + detector for `<verb-converb> ала<person> <ма/ба/па>?` pattern. | v4.13.0 | **Sentence-decomposition foundation + DialogContext multi-turn topic memory + closed-class hygiene** — second minor in the v4.12+ humanness arc. The 2026-05-01 live-REPL transcript surfaced two systemic gaps: greedy first-noun-match (modal particles / negators leaked into noun_hint, surfacing poetry) and goldfish memory (only one back-reference tracked, multi-turn anaphora failed). v4.13.0 lays foundation for both. **Architectural addition #1** — `crates/adam-dialog/src/sentence_decomp.rs` (~470 lines): the Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition; FST already gives us case markers, downstream finally USES them. `SentenceType` + `Role` (11 variants) + `SentenceDecomposition` + `decompose(input, parses, last_topic)` — pure function, O(n), microseconds, zero ML. Case→Role table is the linguistically standard Kazakh grammar (Nominative→Subject, Accusative→Object, Locative→Locus, Ablative→Source, Dative→Recipient, Genitive→Possessor, Instrumental→Instrument). Question-word focus override drives planner routing on `(SentenceType, question_word, focus_role)` instead of just topic-noun. **Architectural addition #2** — `crates/adam-dialog/src/dialog_context.rs` (~250 lines): `DialogContext { topic_history, last_topic, subject_under_discussion, current_domain }` with capped FIFO + majority-vote subject inference over STICKY_WINDOW=6 turns + domain inference over DOMAIN_WINDOW=4 turns. `resolve_anaphor()` consults sticky subject first, falls back to last_topic. New `Conversation.dialog_context` field updated each turn. **(1)** 8 closed-class additions to `NOT_A_TOPIC` (`әлі/әлде/мүмкін/тағы/жоқ/иә/па/пе` — modal particles + existential negator + completing the question-particle paradigm). **(2)** 12 Acc/Dat/Gen anaphor forms added to `DISCOURSE_ANAPHORS` — pre-v4.13.0 only Loc/Abl cases triggered anaphora resolution. **(3)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: 2 new modules + new `Conversation` field + 12 closed-class + 12 anaphor entries; workspace tests **758→777 passing** (+19). Probabilistic suffix-chain prior (`P(suffix_chain)`, natural `root + function^n` learning) reserved for v4.15+; v4.13.0 is purely structural foundation. | v4.6.0 | **Self-awareness layer + discourse anaphora + closed-class hygiene** — fourth v4.x minor. Real-REPL 2026-04-29 transcript surfaced 6 distinct defects + a strategic ask: "make adam understand he's an entity with a name, knowledge, and abilities — and that he should know what he can and cannot do yet". All landed in one release. **Self-awareness**: 3 new `SystemAspect` enum variants (`Capabilities`, `Knowledge`, `Limitations`) + 3 new `SystemIdentity` summary fields (substantial Kazakh prose) + 3 new template families (`ask_about_system.capabilities` / `.knowledge` / `.limitations`). «Не істей аласың?» → adam lists capabilities; «Не білесің?» → adam lists world_core domains; «Нені істей алмайсың?» → adam states limitations honestly (Kazakh-only, no novel generation, no online learning, no internet, no multimedia, no math, admits ignorance). Limitations detector gated on interrogative marker so declarative criticism («сен ештеңе білмейсің») does NOT route there (preserves v4.4.10 Tentative floor). **Discourse anaphora**: new `crates/adam-dialog/src/discourse.rs` module + `last_query_topic` session slot. When input contains anaphor («онда / сонда / осында / мұнда / бұнда / одан / содан / бұдан / осыдан»), conversation layer overrides `noun_hint` with previous turn's topic. Real-REPL «Қазақстан туралы …» → «Ал онда қанша аймақ бар?» now answers «Қазақстанның аймақтары — 17 облыс пен 3 республикалық маңызы бар қала» instead of «Он — сан». **Closed-class hygiene**: NOT_A_TOPIC adds `өте` / `жалпы` (intensifier/scope adverbs) + bare numeral roots `он` / `сон` (FST misanalysis of discourse `онда / сонда`). **Compound self-intro**: `өзіңіз туралы айт` opener triggers AskAboutSystem(General). **Landmarks fact**: new world_core entry «Қазақстандағы көрікті жерлер мен табиғи орындар: Бурабай, Шарын каньоны, Хан Тәңірі, …». Cognitive 59/59→**63/63**, REPL replay 43/43→**50/50**, workspace 693→**703**, template families 50→**53**, `SystemAspect` variants 4→**7**, world_core 947/1116→**949/1120**. Carry-forward to v4.6.1+: «Қандай салаларды білесіз?» (currently routes to Unknown topic-query rather than Knowledge aspect). Why minor: 3 new `SystemAspect` enum variants + 1 new module (`discourse.rs`) + 1 new session-state slot + 3 new SystemIdentity fields — multiple architectural type-system additions | 703 (+10 tests) |
| v4.5.0 | **`Case::LocativeAttributive` FST morphotactics rule** — third v4.x minor. Replaces the v4.4.12 string-side fallback with proper FST native handling of the Kazakh locative-attributive derivation `-дағы / -дегі / -тағы / -тегі`. New `Case::LocativeAttributive` enum variant in `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/morphotactics.rs` + new `LOCATIVE_ATTRIBUTIVE` suffix template `-{D}{A}{G}{I}` covering all four allomorphs (back-voiced / front-voiced / back-voiceless / front-voiceless) via the existing archiphoneme machinery — no per-allomorph branching needed. | v4.4.13 | **Lexicon hygiene patch: multi-POS homonym dedup + missing core nouns + `best_noun_hint` reorder** — closes both v4.4.12 carry-forward defects. **(1)** Pre-v4.4.13 `Lexicon::load` deduplicated by surface root via `HashMap<String, RootEntry>`, so multi-POS homonyms like `тау` (verb_tau + noun_apt_tau) silently lost one reading and the FST analyser saw only the wrong POS. Fix: separate `entries_ordered` (full union of curated + apertium files, dedup only by `id + part_of_speech` to handle exact-copy entries) from `by_surface` (lossy single-POS lookup unchanged). The FST analyser iterates `entries_ordered` and now produces multi-POS analyses. **(2)** Three core nouns absent from the lexicon entirely — `су` (water), `от` (fire), `ер` (saddle / man-as-hero). Added to `data/tokenizer/segmentation_roots.json`. **(3)** Knock-on: v4.4.13's lexicon-dedup fix unblocked `таулар → тау +Plural` parsing, which made `first_noun_root` start returning `тау` and masked the locative-attributive signal on questions like `Қазақстандағы таулар қандай?`. Reordered `best_noun_hint` to run `locative_attributive_hint` immediately after `topic_marker_hint` (before `multiword_entity_hint` / `first_noun_root`) — the `-дағы` morpheme is a strong topic-narrowing signal semantically equivalent to a `туралы` marker. All 5 listing-style questions now answer correctly with both locative (`Қазақстанда қандай таулар бар?`) and locative-attributive (`Қазақстандағы таулар қандай?`) phrasings. 2 new e2e regressions (multi-POS homonym lock + core-noun lock) + 3 REPL replay dialogs (rivers / lakes / deserts via locative-attributive). Cognitive 59/59 unchanged (locking at REPL replay layer), REPL replay 40/40→**43/43**, workspace 690→**692**. | v4.4.5 | **Real-dialog adequacy fixes: CheckContradiction renderer + AskAge self-recall** — Codex external review (2026-04-27 live REPL) caught two v4.4.0 defects the internal suite missed. **(1)** `Action::CheckContradiction` rendered as a confirmation: action layer correctly chose CheckContradiction after `Астана/Алматы`, but the planner kept keying on `intent_key(StatementOfLocation) = "statement_of_location"` and emitted «Алматыда екеніңізді есте сақтаймын», committing to one of the contested values. v4.4.0's dismiss/cap escape hatches were thus answering a question the user never saw asked. | v4.4.0 | **Belief-poisoning recovery: `Action::DismissContradiction` + contradiction-priority cap (Phase 2 Track C)** — closes the post-v4.3.2 "no clean exit" failure mode where `BeliefState.contradictions` non-empty for *any* reason (real conflict, transient typo, parse glitch) clamped every subsequent `ActionPlanner.plan(...)` step 1 to `CheckContradiction` with no escape. Two complementary hatches: **(1) explicit user-initiated dismissal** — new `BeliefState::dismiss_contradiction(subject, predicate)` (symmetric to v4.1.0 `resolve_contradiction`) marks both contested facts `FactStatus::Superseded` + drops `BeliefConflict` + clears `ContradictionToResolve` pending; new `Conversation::try_dismiss_pending_contradiction(input)` fires only when contradictions non-empty AND input matches one of 9 KZ triggers (`екеуі де жоқ`, `екеуі де емес`, `ешқайсысы дұрыс емес`, `білмеймін`, `өткізіп жібер`, `маңызды емес`, `жадтан өшір`, `ұмыт`, `аластат`); runs *before* `try_resolve_pending_contradiction` so "білмеймін" doesn't accidentally pick a candidate; absorption is skipped on a hit; planner short-circuited with direct `ActionPlan::new(Action::DismissContradiction, OutputKind::SocialPleasantry, ...)`; new `__dismiss_contradiction__` marker slot routes planner to dedicated `dismiss_contradiction` template family with 4 KZ variants; new `Action::DismissContradiction` variant (8→9), `Verifier` non-evidence-required + `OutputKind::SocialPleasantry`, `UncertaintyPolicy → EpistemicStatus::Certain`. **(2) implicit time-bounded priority cap** — new `ActionPlanner::CONTRADICTION_PRIORITY_TURNS = 3` const + new `plan_with_turn(intent, belief, task, current_turn)` API (legacy `plan(...)` still wraps `plan_inner(..., None)` for callers without turn id); `Conversation::turn_with_trace` now passes `self.turn_counter`; step 1 of `plan_inner` checks `current_turn.saturating_sub(detected_at_turn) < K` instead of "any contradiction dominates forever," so a conflict logged at turn `T` dominates `T`/`T+1`/`T+2` and falls through on `T+3`; the conflict stays in `belief.contradictions` for audit, only planner priority changes. **Tests**: 3 unit tests for `dismiss_contradiction` (supersedes-all / no-op when empty / slot stays writable), 3 e2e regressions (`dismiss_contradiction_clears_both_cities_on_neither_reply`, `dismiss_contradiction_handles_dont_know_phrasing`, `contradiction_priority_cap_lets_user_move_on`), 2 new cognitive scenarios in new `contradiction_recovery` category. | v4.3.2 | **Critical fix: phantom-city false positive + intelligence roadmap** — real test dialog (2026-04-26) showed the dialog locked into permanent CheckContradiction after a benign AI-modeling profession statement. Root cause: `token_mentions_generic_place` used `token.contains(stem)`; the 2-letter stem `ел` is a substring of `интеллект`, so `recover_named_place_before_generic_location` promoted `жасанды` to a city, the belief layer logged `(USER, city, Жасанды)` against `(USER, city, Атырау)`, planner blocked every subsequent topic. Fix: switch substring → prefix match (`token.starts_with(stem)`) for both `token_mentions_generic_place` and `token_mentions_geo_descriptor`. Captures every real Kazakh word formation (`қалада`, `ауылдан`, `елде`) without false positives on intra-word substrings (`интеллект`, `келдім`, `белгі`). Cognitive baseline: 41/41 → **42/42 canonical**. 656 tests (+1 end-to-end regression `jasandi_intellekt_does_not_break_dialog_with_false_city`, +1 cognitive `occupation_with_intellekt_does_not_create_phantom_city`). | v4.1.2 | **Tools as execution, step 2 (reasoning path)** — second v4.1.x patch. Same pattern as v4.1.1, applied to reasoning. Pre-v4.1.2 `inject_reasoning_chain` did its own filter + score + IsA-depth tiebreak + render; audit-mode `Tool::dispatch(RunLocalReasoner)` shadowed it with a simpler "top 3 triples" picker that had no IsA-depth knowledge — could disagree on tie-breaks. | v4.1.1 | **Tools as execution, step 1 (retrieval path)** — first v4.1.x patch. Begins the tools-as-execution migration. Pre-v4.1.1 `inject_retrieval_example` called `MorphemeIndex::rank` directly; the audit-mode `Tool::dispatch(SearchRetrieval)` shadowed it with a duplicate call that used a hardcoded `RankConfig::default()` instead of the conversation's actual `rank_config`. Now `inject_retrieval_example` *is* the tool dispatch: `ToolContext` gains `rank_config: Option<&RankConfig>`; `Tool::SearchRetrieval` honours it; `inject_retrieval_example` calls `Tool::dispatch(SearchRetrieval { morphemes })`, takes first finding, falls back to v1.6.5 single-morpheme postings lookup if empty, returns `ToolResult` for the caller to record on `TurnTrace.tool_calls`. | v4.0.36 | **Cognitive Eval Harness fixes (Codex v4.0.35 review)** — two harness fixes before Phase 6 builds on top. Codex correctly flagged both as load-bearing weaknesses. **Fix #1 (gate hole)**: pre-v4.0.36 cognitive_eval silently `return`-ed when lexicon/dataset missing — test stayed green without running. Now both loaders use `assert!` / `panic!` — missing inputs fail red. `load_lexicon` returns `LexiconV1` (not Option), dataset read panics with explicit message, empty-dataset case asserted. **Fix #2 (unimplemented contract)**: v4.0.35 docs/roadmap promised `expected_failing: true` aspirational marker — schema didn't have it. Now full implementation: `Scenario.expected_failing: bool` (#[serde(default)]), harness tracks canonical (must pass) and aspirational (can fail, passes are "ready to promote") separately. Report shows both slices with category breakdown. **Two aspirational scenarios added** documenting v4.0.35 findings: `aspirational_unparseable_input_distinguished_from_unknown_topic` (system can't tell "topic without evidence" from "input that doesn't parse"), `aspirational_contradiction_resolution_via_user_choice` (user saying «астанада дұрыс» after CheckContradiction doesn't resolve the conflict). Both fail today; their PASSes will signal Phase 6/7 unlocks. **No production code changed** — only test harness + dataset | 566 tests (unchanged total) |
| v4.0.35 | **Cognitive Eval Harness (Codex roadmap Phase 7a, narrow)** — seventh patch. **Narrow Phase 7 BEFORE Phase 6** per Codex sequencing — lock in measurement baseline across 5 phases before adding tools. **New dataset** `data/eval/cognitive_dialog_dataset.json` — 20 scenarios across 6 categories (goal_continuity 3, topic_switch 3, contradiction_handling 3, action_routing 4, verification_gating 3, epistemic_routing 4). | v4.0.32 | **Verifier + first real output gate (Codex v4.0.26 roadmap Phase 4)** — fourth architectural patch on v5.0 roadmap. **FIRST phase that actually changes user-visible output** — prior phases (1-3) were substrate. **New `crates/adam-dialog/src/verifier.rs`** (~380 lines, 11 unit tests). | v4.0.30 | **Turn-counter fix + ReadyToAnswer reachability (Codex v4.0.29 review)** — two invariant fixes on Phase 2 substrate before Phase 3 builds on top. **#1 (High, Codex)**: pre-v4.0.30 turn ids came from `intent_history.len()` which caps at `MAX_HISTORY = 32`, so `goal_set_at_turn` / `recorded_at_turn` / `detected_at_turn` plateaued after 32 turns. **Fix**: `Conversation::turn_counter: usize` monotone unbounded counter; threaded into `absorb_entities(intent, turn_id)` and `task.roll_forward(..., turn_id)`; saturating-add; cleared on reset. | v4.0.29 | **TaskState + Goal detection (Codex v4.0.26 roadmap Phase 2)** — second architectural patch on v5.0 roadmap. | v4.0.28 | **BeliefState single-active-fact invariant fix (Codex v4.0.27 review #1)** — Codex's v4.0.27 external review found a real invariant bug in the Phase 1 substrate before Phase 2 could start. **Bug**: sequence `value → same value → different value` left the first copy `Active`, so `active_fact()` returned a stale winner even after a contradiction was logged. Pre-v4.0.28 `record_user_fact` used `rposition` and flipped only the most recent active fact. Blocker for Phase 2+ because TaskState / ActionPlanner / Verifier will trust `active_fact()` as authoritative. **Fix**: rewrote to snapshot every prior `Active` fact for `(subject, predicate)` and flip all in one sweep. New invariant enforced by construction — at most one `Active` per `(subject, predicate)` at any time. **Tests**: renamed + tightened `repeated_same_value_preserves_single_active_invariant` (was: both Active, now: fact[0] Superseded + fact[1] Active); new unit `same_same_different_leaves_no_active_fact` (Codex's exact repro) — asserts `active_fact() == None` + 0 active + 1 conflict; new integration `same_same_different_city_leaves_no_active_fact_via_conversation` through full `Conversation::turn` pipeline | 505 tests (+2 invariant regression) |

| v4.0.24 | **Reranker tie-break fix (Codex v4.0.23 re-review #1)** — first patch on Codex's repeat external review. v4.0.22 scorer produced ties that canonical-triple tie-break resolved to semantically weaker candidates. | v4.0.8 | **`extract_facts --world-core-only` fast-path — throughput infrastructure** — one-time patch closing the main inefficiency the user flagged at v4.0.7 ("2 часа на один патч сильно расточительно"). Previous v4.0.3 → v4.0.7 each spent ~45 min on a full 200k-sample text-pack re-extract that produced the same text-facts every time and only differed in the `world_core/` slice. New `--world-core-only` flag on `extract_facts`: (1) read committed `facts.json`, (2) `retain` every fact whose `source.pack` does NOT start with `world_core/`, (3) re-load `data/world_core/*.jsonl` via existing `load_world_core_facts`, (4) merge + recompute `by_predicate` / `by_pack` from scratch, (5) stamp `status: "world_core_refresh"` (new sentinel value, first-class per v3.1.0 iteration contract). Mutually exclusive with `--full` / `--bench-order` / `--max-total` (fails fast). **Measured equivalence**: baseline v4.0.7 `facts.json` (2 476 s elapsed) vs fast-path output — byte-identical save for `status` + `elapsed_s` (both intentional markers). Every one of 13 745 facts, every count, every source chain match exactly. **Measured throughput**: full extract ~41 min (2 476 s) → fast-path <1 s (2.5 s with cargo startup) = **~1 500× speedup** on world_core-only patches. Unblocks the "batch 3–5 domains per patch" direction the user flagged at v4.0.7: 5 domains rebuild in seconds instead of 4 × 45 min = 3 h of serial re-extraction. Guardrail: correct ONLY when text-extraction output is unchanged — any patch touching pattern matchers, lexicon, or corpus MUST still run a full extract. Single-concern patch: one flag, one helper, zero extractor changes, zero new predicates, **463 tests (unchanged — correctness baseline preserved)** | 463 tests (unchanged); first tooling-throughput patch in v4.x, enables axis-rotation rhythm at sustainable cost |

| v4.0.6 | **Narrow attributive blocklist in `is_closed_class`** — continuation of the v4.0.5 noise-elimination axis. v4.0.5 rightmost-subject fix handled multi-head NP cases; this one handles the **head-elided attributive** case («Бірінші дүниежүзілік соғыстан кейін …» → the head noun «соғыс» is consumed as the ablative object, leaving only `дүниежүзілік` as a nominative candidate). Fix: add 9 attributive / fragment roots to `is_closed_class` so every matcher rejects them as subjects. Specifically: **`дүниежүзілік`** (41 After facts), **`ұзақ`** (9), **`әскери`** (6), **`ядролық`** (3), **`тропикалық`** (2), **`жыныстық`** (2), plus fragment parses `жарт` (3), `арасындағ` (4), and the adverb `тағы` (3). **Non-inclusions protected by regression test**: `ұлт-азаттық` (real compound noun), `белгі` / `сан` / `жұрт` (legitimate nouns) all continue to pass. **Measured**: facts **13 887 → 13 703 (−184)**, After **269 → 219 (−50)** (primary target), cross-matcher cleanup — DoesTo **−97**, GoesTo **−22**, RelatedTo **−9**. All 9 blocked roots verified at 0 facts on the committed runtime (spot-check per root). Graph **3 287 → 3 284** nodes, **12 439 → 12 308** edges (−131). Derivations **7 293 → 7 311** (+18 net, structural — R8 and R7 marginally freed by smaller dedup set). Intent-level precision win is substantial even though raw derivation count barely moves: every blocked fact was attributive-as-subject, semantically meaningless | 463 tests (+1 from v4.0.5) |

Fix: **rightmost subject** (closer to verb in Kazakh SOV) + 3-char root minimum. **Measured**: R8 derivations 789 → **714 (−75, −9.5 %)**, total derivations 7 368 → **7 293**; `(тропикалық, After, *)` class base facts 2 → 1 with all transitive multiplications eliminated. **Honest observation**: larger adjacent noise class remains — attributive `-лық`/`-лік`/`-и` adjective-derivations (`дүниежүзілік` 41 facts, `ядролық`, `әскери`, `ұзақ`, `ұлт-азаттық`, `жыныстық`) where FST tags them as nouns and the real subject of «X attributive HEAD-ablative кейін …» is elided because HEAD gets consumed as the ablative object. | v3.8.5 | **Precision hardening — Codex review response (scaling ladder step 8.5)** — patch release closing three categories of defect the external reviewer flagged on v3.8.0. **(1) Doc drift**: removed contradicting README row (`4/5 active rules` vs `3 (R1/R2/R5)` in the same table); architecture_v3 matcher table rewritten from 4 matchers to 11, R3 marked `active (v3.5.5)`, added R6/R7 as v3.9+ targets. **(2) Renderer morphology**: `render_derivation_as_kazakh` (both in `conversation` and in `adam_inspect`) was dash-concatenating case suffixes — `format!("{}-ға", root)` — producing invalid Kazakh like `атау-ға` (broken dash AND front-harmony roots stuck with back -ға). v3.8.5 routes every case suffix through `synthesise_noun(root, features)` so атау→атауға, өсімдік→өсімдікке, қазақ→қазаққа (with gemination). Regression test asserts positive FST form + negative dash absence. Known limitation discovered: FST genitive-after-vowel produces `қаладың` instead of `қаланың` (deep phonology defect deferred to v3.9); renderer sidesteps by using dative/ablative in PartOf/Causes chains. **(3) Matcher precision**: added `is_location_root` (50-toponym allow-list) + `is_time_noun` (22 time words) + expanded `is_closed_class` with `мұндай/сондай/ондай/кейбір/өз/өзі/…`. Refuses country subjects for LivesIn (Қазақстан can't reside), time-noun subjects for LivesIn/GoesTo/DoesTo (күн → goes_to → жұмыс was 16.6 % of all GoesTo), demonstrative subjects across the board. Also rejects LivesIn/GoesTo objects whose FST analysis retains a P3 possessive (fragment parses like `аумағын`). Minimum subject-root length 3 chars. **(4) Demo preview/actual mismatch**: `adam_demo` Part 4 preview claimed `неміс → халқы` but rendered `неміс → ара`. Root cause: demo selected by BTreeMap(rule_id) but `inject_reasoning_chain` used `find(subj==probe || obj==probe)`. Fixed both sides — `inject_reasoning_chain` now strict subject-first two-pass; demo skips derivations whose subject was claimed by an earlier derivation in storage order. 7 new tests (423 total, from 416) | 423 workspace tests (+7); precision + auditability bumped to make v3.9 investor demos credible |

| v3.4.0 | **Lexicon mining pipeline (scaling ladder step 4)** — unblocks the most-multiplicative axis: Lexicon coverage. | v3.3.0 | **Codex polish + precision audit + gold-corpus pilot (scaling ladder step 3)** — response to second Codex external review of v3.2.0, plus first quality-gated ingestion of natural Kazakh corpus beyond wiki/wikisource (3 secondary-school textbooks OCR'd via `tesseract-kaz`). **Codex findings resolved**: (1) weak in-process determinism test strengthened with cross-root-ambiguity expected-order assertions (`кітабы` first vs `кітап`, non-decreasing by root) that fail ≈ 50% of runs on pre-v3.2.0 HashMap-values code; (2) `run_tier` made budget-aware via `run_tier_with_budget` + `EXTRACT_CHUNK_SIZE=128` chunks (SIGINT / `--time-budget` interrupts within ~1 s even inside long T4/T5); (3) doc contradiction in `adam-scaling/lib.rs` reconciled; (4) README `Current state` header refreshed to v3.3.0. **Normalized metrics** (Codex #4 follow-up): new `NormalizedMetrics` on every `ScalingPoint` — `facts_per_10k_words`, `derivations_per_fact`, `predicate_coverage_pct`, `duplicate_fact_rate_pct` — raw counts growing the curve, ratios saying *what kind* of growth it is. **Precision audit** (Codex #3 follow-up): new `audit_precision` bin deterministically samples 50 facts + 50 derivations seed-reproducible to `docs/precision_audit.md` with per-item checkboxes, sentence + pattern + rule, Tally section for native-speaker review. **Gold-corpus pilot**: new OCR pipeline (pdftoppm @ 200 DPI → tesseract-kaz, 6-way parallel) because `pdftotext` drops Қ/Ң/Ғ/Ө/Ү/Ұ/Һ on textbook PDFs with custom font encoding; new `adam-corpus::process_kazakh_textbooks` bin; 3 language-focused books OCR'd (108 913 raw words → **8 421 samples** in `kazakh_textbooks_pack.json`, 2.8 MB committed, per-book provenance). **Scaling T3_10k → T4_50k on new 4.32 M-word pool**: ×5 words → 19→**120 facts** (×6.32), 0→**51 derivations** (super-linear), 38→123 nodes, 19→87 edges (graph densifying). ## Pre-Phase-10 — transformer era (v0.1.0 → v0.4.0)

Historical context for readers who want the full lineage. None of the code or data on this path is load-bearing for v1.0.0 except where explicitly referenced (the v0.4.0 checkpoint, the corpus packs consumed by `validate_foundation.sh`).

- **Phase 6 (v0.1.1 – v0.1.6)** — authentic Kazakh source ingestion: Tatoeba (4,058), Kazakh Wikipedia (15,000), Common Voice KK (6,108). Unified corpus reaches 39 k samples, lossless tokenization at 0 unknowns / 100% roundtrip.
- **Phase 7 (v0.1.3 – v0.2.0)** — transformer baselines on real text. 4.28 M-parameter envelope saturates by v0.2.0 (PPL ~1100 flat); capacity, not data, is the bottleneck.
- **Phase 8 (v0.3.0)** — scale to 20 M params. First non-flat PPL delta since real-text onset (PPL 871). 20 M is the largest config fitting M2 8 GB unified memory.
- **Phase 9 (v0.4.0)** — 24.2 M transformer with literary sources (Abai Wikisource 2,253 samples) + CC-100 web-crawl (50 k filtered) + synthetic-generator min-length raised to 3 words + BPE vocab 4k → 8k. Val PPL 1691.89 on 12,101 held-out samples. Confirmed capacity limit: 24 M × 4 M tokens is ≈ 25× below Chinchilla-optimal.

The post-v0.4.0 pivot was a deliberate choice: further transformer scaling required an order-of-magnitude more data that didn't exist for Kazakh at the quality bar required. The deterministic FST + dialog path delivered MVP-grade predictable Kazakh in pure Rust on the same hardware.

## Post-v1.0 direction

Post-v1.0.0 testing exposed that the MVP was a programmed toy — it answered only the 25 scenarios we enumerated, with no generalisation. The user approved a honest course correction and a long-term commitment to a truly thinking Kazakh model.

### Course-correction rationale

- **v0.9.6 multilingual was a mistake.** The Russian / English triggers diluted the Kazakh-first thesis. A Russian speaker writing "Я разработчик" got "түсінбедім" because "разработчик" wasn't in the Lexicon — the recogniser widened the surface without adding real coverage.
- **Fundamental trade-off acknowledged.** Rule-based systems can't generalise; neural systems can but hallucinate. You can't have both. The v1.0.0 predictable pipeline is kept, and generalisation will come as a neural **fallback** for `Intent::Unknown` only — the 26-intent deterministic backbone stays as the 0-hallucination guarantee.

### Committed sequence

- **v1.1.0 (done)** — Kazakh-only revert; modern Lexicon expansion (+12 roots); Insult intent; smart Unknown handler with noun-hint. Incremental coverage without abandoning thesis.
- **v1.x** — Kazakh corpus engineering. **Committed 4.01 M / local 77.9 M as of v1.5.0 (gap to 100 M = 1.3×)**. Target: **100 M+ Kazakh tokens** from native-text sources (Qazaq Wikipedia, literature, government Kazakh, OCR books). v1.5.5 government sources are expected to close the gap. Pure data engineering, not ML.
- **v2.0** — compact Kazakh LM (transformer or SSM), trained in pure Rust (GGML-style, no PyTorch). Plugged in as the `Intent::Unknown` fallback only. The 26-intent pipeline continues to handle everything it recognises at 0 hallucinations.
- **post-v2.0** — multimodality (speech / vision) only after a truly thinking Kazakh LM exists. Not before.

### Post-v1.1.0 candidates (not promised, not scheduled)

- Native-speaker review of the template set (phrasing, register, naturalness).
- Further modern Lexicon expansion (50+ new professions + tech vocabulary).
- Verb slot expansion (`{root|verb_features}` with verb synthesiser dispatch).
- Additional intents beyond the current 26.

## Out of scope (permanent)

- **Multilingual input and output** (v1.1.0 revert). The v0.9.6 Russian / English triggers were removed. `adam` accepts and produces only Kazakh. Generalisation comes via the v2.0 Kazakh LM, not translation.
- **Speech / multimodal** — deferred until a thinking Kazakh LM exists.
- **Cloud platform work.**
- **50 M+ parameter transformer experiments on current hardware** (M2 8 GB). Target for v2.0 is a compact model that fits on this hardware.
- **Probabilistic / LLM-style free generation in the recognised-intent path.** The 26-intent deterministic backbone never hallucinates. Only the `Unknown`-fallback path (v2.0) is allowed to be generative, and responses from that path will be explicitly marked in traces.
